         <section class="rsttop-othersearch">
          <h2 class="rsttop-heading1">
           
          </h2>
          <div class="rsttop-othersearch__list-wrap">
           <ul class="rsttop-othersearch__photolist">
            <li class="rsttop-othersearch__photolist-item rsttop-othersearch__photolist-item--kodawari07">
             <p class="rsttop-othersearch__photolist-item-img">
              <img alt="" src="images/restaurant/image/kodawari_index_7.jpg"/>
             </p>
             <a class="js-analytics rsttop-othersearch__photolist-target" data-analytics-btn="TOP_cond__" href="https://tabelog.com/rstLst/?ChkSanitation=1">
              <div class="rsttop-othersearch__photolist-wrap">

    var cookie = this.convert();

  },
  convert:function(){
    var arr = document.cookie.split(/;\s/),
        item="",
        result={};

      item = arr[index].split("=");
      result[item[0]]=item[1];
    }
    return result;
  },
}
